  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_5ea43879-9981-4d3a-a35b-2dc06014084c'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

The Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse.<br /><br />His name is Ares, and the fate of mankind rests on his powerful shoulders. If he falls to the forces of evil, the world falls too. Not when his own brother plots against him. <br /><br />Yet there is one last hope. Gifted in a way other humans can't-or won't-understand, Cara Thornhart is the key to both this Horseman's safety and his doom. But involving Cara will prove treacherous, even beyond the maddening, dangerous desire that seizes them the moment they meet. For staving off eternal darkness could have a staggering cost: Cara's life.</span>

<div id="review_144681074" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/144681074" />
    <a title="Anzu The Great Destroyer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer"><img alt="Anzu The Great Destroyer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1455829739p2/2278800.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/144681074?book_show_action=true">Jan 30, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anzu The Great Destroyer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anzu The Great Destroyer" href="/user/show/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer">Anzu The Great Destroyer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/9860733-eternal-rider">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">fans of the genre, series, author, etc</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=reviewed-2011">reviewed-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=romance-paranormal">romance-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=zomg-i-must-have-him">zomg-i-must-have-him</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=evil-satan">evil-satan</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=holy-winged-ones">holy-winged-ones</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer144681074" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6493986691314601718">Let’s start with the cover(s). Why do PNR books (almost) always have on them the half-naked hot dude who’s missing half of his face? There was a time when I didn’t really mind it but enough already! See the UK version for this book? <b>AWESOME!</b> I really REALLY love it! And I saw many book covers from the UK which were pretty good which means that the trends are different there. Anyways, I’m hoping that US books, especially from this genre, will change the cover style a bit because this isn’t hot an</span>
  <span id="freeText6493986691314601718" style="display:none">Let’s start with the cover(s). Why do PNR books (almost) always have on them the half-naked hot dude who’s missing half of his face? There was a time when I didn’t really mind it but enough already! See the UK version for this book? <b>AWESOME!</b> I really REALLY love it! And I saw many book covers from the UK which were pretty good which means that the trends are different there. Anyways, I’m hoping that US books, especially from this genre, will change the cover style a bit because this isn’t hot anymore.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380344910i/699719._SX540_.jpg" width="450" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I’ve always liked a good Armageddon theme. The story was actually what I loved the most about Eternal Rider. It’ been a while since the last time I’ve read a PNR book and this one seemed good. I’m a real big fan of Larissa Ione and I was sure she wouldn’t disappoint.<br> <br>The whole Apocalypse thing is popular lately so I see Larissa Ione’s decision to shift Demonica into this as a breath of fresh air. I respect the fact that she knew when to take this break and didn’t lengthen Demonica into something… well… sh*tty. Eventually it would have turned out boring, trust me on this one. It helps if you read the whole Demonica series before starting this but I guess you could manage if you didn’t. You’d miss some details but nothing too important.<br><br><b>Twenty ways to f*ck up a human mind</b> – a good title for this book. This poor chick, Cara, is going through a lot of sh*t in Eternal Rider. I never get tired of seeing a human react to the whole <i>“The Boogeyman Is Real”</i> story. What should be the normal reaction to “The Bogeyman Is Real”? This:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380344910i/699720.jpg" width="450" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yep! Eventually she dealt with it and all was fine.<br><br>Ares was a good character. Ever since I watched Xena, 1000 years ago, I got my eyes on Ares. It’s not the same guy but the name makes me think of the actor (don’t know his name, I just know that he died so R.I.P. *sad face*) who was a major hottie/badass/assh*le (and I mean assh*le in a good way).<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380344910i/699721._SX540_.jpg" width="450" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anyways, back to the Ares at hand. I loved those scenes when he went all badass on poor Cara. The girl was a wuss at first so she needed a bit of training. I’ve always admired strong heroines so the thought of Cara being weak and the typical damsel in distress made me worry a bit. She wasn’t the typical strong and ruthless character but she did ok. If she was more than this she’d clash with Ares and they’d up kicking each other’s ass non-stop. No good chemistry there, I’m sure…<br><br>Now u go to Cara and Hal. I’ve always admired characters that can tame beasts and then form that friendship bond that results in love and devotion. I wish I could do that, dammit!!! I want my own hellhound! *sigh*<br><br>Btw wanted to find a great picture of a hellhound and guess what? Didn’t find sh*t. Why the hell is Google out of nice hellhound artwork?!?! This is like provoking me to start working on one. And I will. Later…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380344910i/699722._SX540_.png" width="450" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That’s the best I could find: hellhound sculpture/3D thing. Good for references though…<br><br>Pestilence is one hell of a villain. Even though at first I wasn’t happy about the whole evil brother gig (reminded me too much of Demonica with Rick or whatever his name was (I Googled and it’s Roag) and the other guys) it eventually got better and meaner and bloodier and I have to stop now ‘cause I’m using too many and’s.<br><br>I really love Larissa Ione’s stories. They are always fast paced, they never give you time to get bored. There may be moments where she writes about unnecessary things but they are few and the book as a whole makes it up for them. In Eternal Rider I had some of those moments but in the end the story and characters got to me and I didn’t even remember the boring parts.<br><br>Wraith’s presence was nice also – I really missed the guy.<br><br>Great turn of events in the end. I mean I knew Cara wasn’t going to die but, as always, I was curious how the author will fix her up. I’m proud to say I was close enough. At least I guessed the species that will save her. That’s something.<br><br>And now some extra parts with some spoilers. Just some thoughts. Irrelevant so you may not read if you wish.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Why am I not surprised that Cara is a good and perfect (well, almost perfect) person. She takes pity in things (like transferring the agimortus – or whatever they call it these days – to an asshole angel who called her stupid in her face) and then makes the plot longer and more complicated. I mean yeah why would this be simple? Why would a heroine be simple and say “Hey angel dude! F*ck you! Here’s the damn thing, I hope you choke on it!”? At least that would be me… Wrong thing to do? Yes? Aaah pity then. Btw I know this would have ended up bad in the end but how was I to know?? Pestilence is a genius so he’s tough to predict!<br><br>Great ending even though Ares should have been surer of Cara’s feelings for him. I mean come on surely she loves him so much and will accept marrying him… or wait, women are strange sometimes so she might have said no. I take it back then. But seeing Ares act like a kid was cute. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>Top 5 quotes</b><br><br><b>#5</b><i> “It wasn’t a kiss, human, so don’t get excited.”<br>She sputtered in outrage. “I don’t know what putting your lips on someone else’s mouth means for your people—whatever they are—but humans call that a kiss.”<br>“Congratulations, then. You made out with a hellhound.”</i><br><br><b>#4</b><i> Was he actually looking forward to seeing Cara again? The goofy way his lips were curved into a smile said yes, and horror of horrors, he realized he was experiencing some sort of crush.<br>He needed to kill something. </i><br><br><b>#3</b><i> “I’ve never been in this region before.”<br>Thanatos glanced around. “Me either.”<br>“Maybe because this place sucks.” Wraith flipped a throwing knife from hand to hand. “I thought we were going to get to fight. Talk about lame. I’m seriously disappointed in you Horsemen people.”</i><br><br><b>#2</b><i> One of Than’s vampire servants hustled to clean up Batarel’s remains, and he bowed before Ares. “May I take those body parts from you, sir?”</i><br><br><b>#1</b><i> “Hal… he wouldn’t… I mean, look at him.”<br>Hal leaped into the air, his jaws snapping as he caught a bird he’d flushed. The poor bird was gone in an instant, an explosion of feathers floating around Hal’s head.<br>“Sure,” Ares said wryly. “Look at him.”</i><br><br>Read the review on <a href="http://zombiehazard.blogspot.com/2011/07/eternal-rider-lords-of-deliverance-1.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"></a>ZombieHazard.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1404026544" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1404026544" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1404026544?book_show_action=true">Sep 29, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=angels">angels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=immortals">immortals</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=worldend-endofworldasweknowit">worldend-endofworldasweknowit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=1paranormal-lovestories">1paranormal-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=afterlife">afterlife</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=demons">demons</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1404026544" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7553629197414286206">“Lords of Deliverance” is a spinoff from “Demonica”, but I will always consider them same series. The world is the same. <br/>Demons are still around. Angels, kind of angels, wolves, kind of wolves, vampires and other magnificent beloved monsters are still around. And UGH and Aegis are still around.<br/>It is just now there are also some extra players in the scene. And what outstanding players!<br/><br/><b>The Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse!</b><br/><br/>I mean, think about it. <br/>There is nothing else worse than this complication. W</span>
  <span id="freeText7553629197414286206" style="display:none">“Lords of Deliverance” is a spinoff from “Demonica”, but I will always consider them same series. The world is the same. <br />Demons are still around. Angels, kind of angels, wolves, kind of wolves, vampires and other magnificent beloved monsters are still around. And UGH and Aegis are still around.<br />It is just now there are also some extra players in the scene. And what outstanding players!<br /><br /><b>The Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse!</b><br /><br />I mean, think about it. <br />There is nothing else worse than this complication. We have <br />-Ares (War), <br />-Reseph (Pestilence), <br />-Thanatos (Death), <br />-and the only female of the four, Limos (Famine)<br /><br />The four horsemen are doing exactly what each of their names is saying. But they are really nice guys deep down and they try to avoid bringing disasters. <br /><br />The nicest of them is Reseph. He loves to party, he loves to love. Unfortunately he is also the unluckiest one.<br /><br />If you have read Sin Undone, you will probably know that humankind is in deep sh!t, because Reseph’s seal has been broken. Reseph will not be nice anymore. Pestilence is about to conquer Earth.<br /><br />Yes, the four horsemen come with four seals that they must not be broken. The prophecy of the Apocalypsis is waiting to be fulfilled when all four of the seals are broken. <br /><br />And the beginning of the end is here. Reseph half mad, half determined will try to break the rest of the three seals and bring plagues everywhere in Earth. No more Mr Nice Guy anymore.<br />His brothers and sister will try to stop him. <br /><br />The first book is about immortal horseman Ares (War) and mortal Cara. Ares seal will break if an angel dies. Cara, without realizing it, will receive the seal before this happens and now Ares has to protect her in order to protect the seal. <br />There will be some complications of course. Cara will also be the proud owner of a strange dog, named Hal, after she saves him. Okay, he is not really a dog. <br />What? Did you expect to find a normal dog in the Demonica world? Cara will receive a Hell's Kiss from Hal who is definitely not a dog and who has a very important grandfather old dog.<br /><br />Great world building, awesome new characters, fast pace, nice love story and grand ending!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7553629197414286206" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer60868095479000689">5 stars – Paranormal Romance<br/><br/>What a <b>fan-freaking-tastic</b>, brilliant <i>(Guinness Beer guy voice)</i> combination of unique paranormal elements and apocalyptic prophecies, Stephen King-esque eerie horror, violent, gruesome action, intense, steamy romance, and wry, dark humor. Larissa Ione’s <b>
  <i>Demonica</i>
</b> is one of my top favorite series that got impossibly better with each book, and she really <i>delivers</i> the goods in the first book in the spin-off <b>
  <i>Lords of Deliverance</i>
</b> series. It was an amazing read, and </span>
  <span id="freeText60868095479000689" style="display:none">5 stars – Paranormal Romance<br /><br />What a <b>fan-freaking-tastic</b>, brilliant <i>(Guinness Beer guy voice)</i> combination of unique paranormal elements and apocalyptic prophecies, Stephen King-esque eerie horror, violent, gruesome action, intense, steamy romance, and wry, dark humor. Larissa Ione’s <b>
  <i>Demonica</i>
</b> is one of my top favorite series that got impossibly better with each book, and she really <i>delivers</i> the goods in the first book in the spin-off <b>
  <i>Lords of Deliverance</i>
</b> series. It was an amazing read, and I can’t wait for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9868970.Immortal_Rider__Lords_of_Deliverance___2_" title="Immortal Rider (Lords of Deliverance, #2) by Larissa Ione" rel="nofollow noopener">Immortal Rider</a>! Big 5 stars! <br /><br />This was one of my favorite lines.<br /><br /><i>It was a real fun stew of what-the-fuck.</i></span>

<div id="review_118760154" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/118760154" />
    <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352609417p2/2489554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/118760154?book_show_action=true">Aug 26, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Demonica fans, paranormal romance fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=first-book-in-series">first-book-in-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=my-hottie-harem">my-hottie-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=king-of-the-harem">king-of-the-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=tortured-bad-boys">tortured-bad-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=gods">gods</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=keep-a-spare-pair-of-knickers">keep-a-spare-pair-of-knickers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer118760154" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18421848734882964270"><b> 4.5 STARS!!!!</b><br/><br/><b>Ares’s To-Do List:<br/>-	Stop (sexy) brother from obliterating the world with deadly disease<br/>-	Find the agimorti and keep her from getting killed<br/>-	Locate the Deliverance before Pestilence finds it</b><br/>[Edited in by Anne:]<br/>-	<b>And learn that having feeeeeeeelings doesn’t make you a pansyass wanker!! </b><br/><br/>I’m a huge fan of the Demonica series so I was thrilled to hear about a new spinoff series with the four horsemen. <i>Eternal Rider</i> has all the same great elements of Demonica. Ione still has her great s</span>
  <span id="freeText18421848734882964270" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 STARS!!!!</b><br /><br /><b>Ares’s To-Do List:<br />-	Stop (sexy) brother from obliterating the world with deadly disease<br />-	Find the agimorti and keep her from getting killed<br />-	Locate the Deliverance before Pestilence finds it</b><br />[Edited in by Anne:]<br />-	<b>And learn that having feeeeeeeelings doesn’t make you a pansyass wanker!! </b><br /><br />I’m a huge fan of the Demonica series so I was thrilled to hear about a new spinoff series with the four horsemen. <i>Eternal Rider</i> has all the same great elements of Demonica. Ione still has her great sense of humor. She has that raw writing style that makes the narration sooo damn good and she’s the shit when it comes to worldbuilding! <br /><br /><b>Ares aka War</b>, the second of the horsemen has a lot to deal with. With his brother, Reseph channelling his evil side as Pestilence, he’s got his hands full with trying to keep him from obliterating the world. I will admit, I liked him in the beginning but then somewhere in the middle, he kind of pissed me off with how he tried to hold himself away from Cara so much, fighting his feelings to the point where I was getting frustrated. You are War! Having feelings doesn’t make you a ninny. It’s okay to feeeeeeeel! But he does get better and I couldn’t be happier with the end results.<br /><br /><b>Cara </b>was a skittish one at first and I was dying for a heroine with a little more backbone. And then suddenly, she grows a pair and learns to cope with the bomb that Ares had dropped on her. I have to respect that. I will admit, I wasn’t feeling the chemistry between Ares and Cara at first. With a few heated glances and one kiss, I was eager for something more to happen. But Ares controls himself so much that there are no opportunities for him to slip his control. And Cara isn’t one to initiate contact.<br /><br />But that doesn’t take away from Ione’s spectacular writing. I love the rawness to it. I especially love the violence in this one! I can’t remember if the Demonica series was as gory and bloody as this one since I read it awhile back, but I LOVE IT! Gory. Bloody. Raw. Love it!<br /><br />And with that, I have to say how much I love <b>Reseph</b>, or rather, Pestilence because his bad side is so much more appealing! Ione writes baddies well! I loved the venom in his tone when he speaks and his merciless outlook on mankind. Pestilence is as badass as they come.<br /><br />Then there’s <b>Reaver</b>, whom I loved from the Demonica series! This Reaver is a little more darker, one whose more irritable and with his evil counterpart Harvester, chaos is bound to find them sooner or later.<br /><br />I’ve mentioned Pestilence already so naturally, that leaves <b>Limos</b> (Famine) and <b>Thanatos</b> (Death)! I LOVE them both! Limos is friggin’ hilarious. She kind of reminds me of the Valkyries from KC’s IAD series. She’s great! And Than is a hottie! A tattooed hottie! I cannot wait for either of their books!<br /><br /><b>For Demonica fans</b>, there’s reason to rejoice because there are familiar faces! Sin is mentioned a few times. Arik, Runa’s brother from the R-XR is present and him and Kynan get real chummy with one another. Gem is there as well and there’s wonderful news for my favourite Goth girl! E, Shade, Wraith, Con and Luc are all there too! It’s one big party!<br /><br />I’m super excited for the next book <i>Immortal Rider</i> which is Arik and Limos’ book! <br /><br />So if you’re unsure about starting this series, please do! It’s great! Just prepare for your world to be rocked, because the <b>Horsemen have arrived!</b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="18421848734882964270" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_123582378" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/123582378" />
    <a title="Katie(babs)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/179852-katie-babs"><img alt="Katie(babs)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1242522005p2/179852.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/123582378?book_show_action=true">Sep 26, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katie(babs)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katie(babs)" href="/user/show/179852-katie-babs">Katie(babs)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer123582378" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14763187552371200139">If I could describe Larissa Ione’s new book, Eternal Rider, in one word, it would be “whoa”, as in this book seriously blew my mind away. Eternal Rider is the first book in Larissa’s Lords of Deliverance series that’s an offshoot of her very popular Demonica series. If you thought Larissa Demonica series was dark, beyond steamy erotic and twisted, you’ll be happy to know that Eternal Rider is all these things and much more. Larissa walks a fine line here because everything is more intense. I cou</span>
  <span id="freeText14763187552371200139" style="display:none">If I could describe Larissa Ione’s new book, Eternal Rider, in one word, it would be “whoa”, as in this book seriously blew my mind away. Eternal Rider is the first book in Larissa’s Lords of Deliverance series that’s an offshoot of her very popular Demonica series. If you thought Larissa Demonica series was dark, beyond steamy erotic and twisted, you’ll be happy to know that Eternal Rider is all these things and much more. Larissa walks a fine line here because everything is more intense. I couldn’t believe how far she went with things. At one point I had to put Eternal Rider down and take a break. I usually don’t do this with the books I read, but the amount of fighting and the eye-popping character’s actions really sucker punches you in the gut.<br /><br />Also Larissa writes one of the most inventive, “did she really do what I think she did?” sex scenes that not only shocked me senseless but was too good for words. Larissa has written an upside down tree sex scene, and no, the heroine and hero don’t have upside down sex with a tree, but with each other (a vine is used in a creative way). For that alone Larissa gets two thumbs up from me. Surprises like this among other jaw dropping scenes makes Eternal Rider a book full of win and one paranormal fiction/romance fans will eat up. If you’re looking for light and fluffy, look elsewhere.<br /><br />Eternal Rider introduces the future Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse. Ares is the hero of this story and the horseman of War. His siblings, Reseph is Pestilence, Thanatos is Death and Limos, their sister is Famine. The only way the end of the days aka the Apocalypse can come to pass is if their seals are broken. As long as none of their seals break, the world is safe. Unfortunately Reseph’s seal breaks and he brings Pestilence across the land. Reseph is now evil incardinate and Ares and his other two siblings must try and stop him.<br /><br />Ares has a past full or heartbreak and woe. He once lived as a human centuries ago before he found out what his destiny was. So much was taken from him and because of it he lives in seclusion with only his servants. He refuses to give into love, but that all changes when Cara Thornhart falls into his life.<br /><br />Cara has a unique way with animals. She can heal them, and because of her ability, she becomes a target. When she tries to heal an injured dog, she’s attacked by scary armed men who use their fists to get the answers they want. The reason is the hurt dog is not a dog at all, but a hellhound Cara names Hal. She’s bonded with Hal by no choice of her own and because of that Ares must protect her. Then a fallen angel transfers something called the agimortus onto Cara. This agirmoty thing, as Cara calls it, gives her unbelievable strength and power, but will end up killing her if she can’t transfer it back to another. Also, if Hal dies, so does she. Not only does Ares have to stop Reseph, but keep Cara away from his deranged brother and every other demon, hellhound and supernatural creature searching for her. Plus Ares can’t keep his libido quiet around Cara, and although he’s willing to act on his desires with her, he refuses to care for her because loving another woman would weaken him.<br /><br />Cara is abused every which way to Sunday and is forced to do so many thing that would make another woman crawl into a corner and rock. She’s forced to accept things, even with Ares, who expects to be obeyed in everything. So much happens to Cara, such as near death, torture, almost rape and mind-numbing sex (thanks to Ares) that had my head spinning. What more could this woman go through that would finally make her break down and turn her into a drooling vegetable?<br /><br />Ares has his ulterior motives as does those he’s involved with. He’s a damaged soul who can’t get over his past. Cara is his savior and the perfect balm to help him move on, if he can. Times are bleak and a HEA for these two may be questionable in the big scheme of things.<br /><br />Even though the majority of Eternal Rider has a large amount of dark undertones, there are some laughs and nice snark, mainly from Limos. There’s this great scene where a fallen angel has been captured and she decides to torture him with Ares’s dvd collection of Miami Vice and Starsky and Hutch. This is an example of a few lighthearted moments that are very much needed.<br /><br />The love scenes are beyond steamy and Larissa raises them up a notch. The moment I read the upside down tree sex between Ares and Cara, I was floored, but in a good way.<br /><br />Eternal Rider is one book that may not be for everyone. But it is one wild ride that I couldn’t’ get enough of. I look forward to the next book in this series, which will be about Limos and how one kiss or being too touchy feely with another man can make her the queen and breeder for Lucifer, the rule of hell. I can pretty much assume that will also be a rip roaring, at times shocking read, but one that I would gladly climb aboard as a passenger of Larissa Ione train.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14763187552371200139" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=authors-i-o">authors-i-o</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer242229039" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15419342563573146625">Three Horsemen & 1 Horsewoman of the Apocalypse…..<blockquote>
  
    <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439137753i/15799668.jpg' alt=' photo Four-Horsemen_zps8ejgzuvk.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  
</blockquote> Only they have the power to start off or prevent Armageddon.<br/><br/>If you are a fan like me, of Larissa Ione’s fantastic Demonica books, you are going to love Lords of Deliverance, the spinoff from that series. It’s a good idea to read the Demonica Series before starting on this one…. Eternal Rider, the 1st book in the LOD series begins just after the end of Sin Undone, when Sin unintentionally initiated the beginning of the apocalypse, aft</span>
  <span id="freeText15419342563573146625" style="display:none">Three Horsemen &amp; 1 Horsewoman of the Apocalypse…..<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439137753i/15799668.jpg" alt=" photo Four-Horsemen_zps8ejgzuvk.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> Only they have the power to start off or prevent Armageddon.<br><br>If you are a fan like me, of Larissa Ione’s fantastic Demonica books, you are going to love Lords of Deliverance, the spinoff from that series. It’s a good idea to read the Demonica Series before starting on this one…. Eternal Rider, the 1st book in the LOD series begins just after the end of Sin Undone, when Sin unintentionally initiated the beginning of the apocalypse, after breaking the first Horsemen seal.<br><br>Get ready to take a thrilling ride to the imaginative, dark, witty, sensual and vivid world that Larissa Ione has created. <br><br>This is Ares, Lord of War’s story. <blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439137753i/15799669.jpg" alt=" photo ab_11_zpsxhc9but9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> Fighting to keep his seal intact and protecting his siblings and not never letting feelings of love ever entering his heart.<br><br>But fate works in very strange ways!!!! Forced to protect Cara, a human who may be the one to either save or destroy him.<br>Cara has a very traumatized past and has no idea of the supernatural world that surrounds her. <blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439137753i/15799670.jpg" alt=" photo 4d76f2b30eafbbff20f10c502512b8f2_zps5u5uvphy.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>She’s quiet, sweet and timid, kind hey is this the kind of heroine I wanted for gorgeous Ares????? But hey, Ares is smitten………even the evil hellhounds who eat anything that comes their way…love her…so how could he resist her???? <blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439137753i/15799671.jpg" alt=" photo 4649160bf0ab4f9320a37a6bbf422f48_zpserkziemk.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> She’s not sure about Ares…he’s arrogant and a total ass….<br>But when she then discovers that she might not have that long to live….….well, why not??? <blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439137753i/15799672.jpg" alt=" photo bc5ce2f3-b147-4728-a921-8345efd65fe2_zpsuljiwwuj.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> I enjoyed the development of Cara and Ares relationship….hell, she almost brings him to his knees…<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439137753i/15799673.jpg" alt=" photo cb15455771d3a49f730b8d8e663544f5_zpse8114qm4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote> Fast paced, multi-layered plot, dark and witty humor, amusing banter,<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439137753i/15799674.jpg" alt=" photo images17_zpsd1e1e841.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>sexy and wicked demons and devils….what more could we ask for??? <br><br>How happier could I be seeing some of the characters I have come to love from the Demonica Series make an appearance or two in this story.<br><br>There was a huge amount of back-story to the Horsemen’s history which dragged on a bit in the beginning, it does set up the world of this series.<br><br>Although the Demonica Series is still my favorite by this author, I did enjoy this book and I am looking forward to Limos book next.<br><br><b>My favorite quote:</b><br><blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1439137753i/15799675.jpg" alt=" photo 086990fd84a1552207e0b2cc20e6effa_zps9ohn3ogr.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3154149897581944104">In this sixth book of the Demonica series, we switch over to the Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse. Eros, or War is after his brother, who has gone from being one of the good guys to Pestilence, and trying to plague humanity. He’s also trying to protect Kara, who has been marked by a fallen Angel and has all sorts of people after her! <br/><br/>I thought the introduction of the Four Horsemen was a cool change in the series, and we still get to see Idolin and the Sem brother gang pop in from time to time. Th</span>
  <span id="freeText3154149897581944104" style="display:none">In this sixth book of the Demonica series, we switch over to the Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse. Eros, or War is after his brother, who has gone from being one of the good guys to Pestilence, and trying to plague humanity. He’s also trying to protect Kara, who has been marked by a fallen Angel and has all sorts of people after her! <br /><br />I thought the introduction of the Four Horsemen was a cool change in the series, and we still get to see Idolin and the Sem brother gang pop in from time to time. This book incorporates lots of animals, including hell-hounds, which was really cute. All in all, a great continuation of the series! <br /><br />Please excuse typos/name misspellings. Entered on screen reader.<br /></span>

<div id="review_109568584" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/109568584" />
    <a title="Danielle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3085379-danielle"><img alt="Danielle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415978472p2/3085379.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/109568584?book_show_action=true">Jul 01, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Danielle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Danielle" href="/user/show/3085379-danielle">Danielle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer109568584" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11096480521449738991">Larissa Ione has a new series out and it's not only dark and exciting but hot and adventurous. Her Demonica series was not just mouthwatering but quickly became one of my favorites. I was super excited to find out this new book would be set in the same world as Demonica. Please welcome the Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse. Ares (War), Reseph (Pestilence), Thanatos (Death), and the only female in the group, Limos (Famine). Each of the Horsemen have a Seal and each Seal comes with two prophecies. T</span>
  <span id="freeText11096480521449738991" style="display:none">Larissa Ione has a new series out and it's not only dark and exciting but hot and adventurous. Her Demonica series was not just mouthwatering but quickly became one of my favorites. I was super excited to find out this new book would be set in the same world as Demonica. Please welcome the Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse. Ares (War), Reseph (Pestilence), Thanatos (Death), and the only female in the group, Limos (Famine). Each of the Horsemen have a Seal and each Seal comes with two prophecies. The goal will be keeping these seals intact so the end of the world doesn't come. Unfortunately, that might be a little too late for Reseph. His Seal has broke and this brother is now causing disease and plagues all across the world. Can he be stopped in time?<br /> <br /><br />Cara has the secret ability to heal animals, although she is not a practicing vet she tries to help and is thrown into a whole new world when an injured dog is brought to her doorstep. Just to add to this mess she then comes to find out, well, this isn't just a regular dog. Of course not it is a hellhound. Since she has no idea what in the world a hellhound actually is, but he bonds with her. Ares’ seal is passed over to Cara. Normally humans arent strong enough to carry Seals, but since she is now bonded to the hellhound, she is alive for the time being and Ares must make sure Cara stays that way. If not and his Seal is to break, he will become War and the world as she has come to know it will never be the same. <br /><br /> <br /><br />Getting into this book way never an issue. It was the same world but different main characters who by the end of book I loved. These new characters are not only interesting but I loved that they had a good and bad side to them. And you get to see both sides. *squee* As in any new book of series the information and rules are very detailed and tend to overwhelm you while you are trying to get lost in this world. Even though a lot of information is thrown at you, I loved how you are reminded through out the book so you never can forget what they are. Once you pass through the beginning of the book it turns into smooth sailing from there and you wont be able to put down this tasty treat.<br /><br /> <br />I loved Ares! I mean the way his character is and comes undone with Cara was not only sweet but sigh worthy. He for sure had his swooning moments. The build up to their relationship was not overly done and just perfect. The sex scenes are hot. I also loved that the characters from the Demonica series made some guest appearances. That was a great treat getting to see them and how their lives have turned out since that series ended.<br /><br />I will have to recommend this book to everyone. It was a breath of fresh air. Larissa Ione never disappoints and she will have you hooked. I cant wait for the second book in the series Immortal Rider which is set to release December 2011.<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11096480521449738991" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_141588476" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/141588476" />
    <a title="Leah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3050338-leah"><img alt="Leah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474253068p2/3050338.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/141588476?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Leah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Leah" href="/user/show/3050338-leah">Leah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3050338-leah?shelf=m-f">m-f</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3050338-leah?shelf=adult-lit">adult-lit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3050338-leah?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer141588476" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11570095096592511998">First, I just wanted to say how cool it was that Larissa Ione thanked her Twitter, FB, and GR friends in her acknowledgements because I was like, "Hey, that's me!" It was quite exciting.<br/><br/>So, the book started out just a little bit slow for me. I'm not exactly sure why, but it did, but I wasn't concerned because I knew I'd get into it. Then, it got really good and I started loving it. I was all over Ares and how sexy he was, and Cara and how awesome she was, and Kynan and how awesome I already knew</span>
  <span id="freeText11570095096592511998" style="display:none">First, I just wanted to say how cool it was that Larissa Ione thanked her Twitter, FB, and GR friends in her acknowledgements because I was like, "Hey, that's me!" It was quite exciting.<br /><br />So, the book started out just a little bit slow for me. I'm not exactly sure why, but it did, but I wasn't concerned because I knew I'd get into it. Then, it got really good and I started loving it. I was all over Ares and how sexy he was, and Cara and how awesome she was, and Kynan and how awesome I already knew he was, etc., etc., etc. Then...it started pissing me off quite a bit. Not the plot, because I thought the plot was actually really great, but a certain character.<br /><br />I can't stand Cara. Which saddens me. I originally really liked her! Buuuut...I stopped liking her so much when she refused to transfer the <i>agimortus</i> to the Unfallen angel. What! I do not give a damn if you don't like violence, don't want to violate him, blah blah blah. If you so are so against violence, then why the hell wouldn't you transfer it to someone who was actually meant to carry the <i>agimortus</i> instead of being an idiot and holding on to it when you are going to die in a matter of days? When your freaking death will start freaking Armageddon?! The biggest war of all?! How is that even logical? HOW?! So, she refused to transfer it and it was all, "Good morning, Vietnam!" Except ten times worse. So, it was all downhill from there with me and Cara, and everything she did pissed me off.<br /><br />Like with Cara, I started out loving Ares. <i>Loved him.</i> However, once I stopped liking Cara, I stopped loving Ares so much. I just...he freaking worshipped the ground she walked on and I just couldn't handle that. I mean, I still think he's sexy as hell and I still really like him, but I think he's an idiot.<br /><br />On the bright side! I really, <i>really</i> loved seeing Wraith, Ky (Aw, he's a daddy!), Shade, Gem, Eidolon, and Arik. (Tayla not so much since I still don't like her.) It was really great to see them all again. It was like a big family reunion! *sniffle sniffle weep weep* I loved the character Hades and I look forward to seeing where Ione goes with him. Thanatos, even though he annoyed me sometimes, was extremely sexy. All those tattoos and piercings...*swoon!* I absolutely adored Limos and she is my favorite of the Horsemen. I cannot wait for her book! And I'm super psyched because it comes out on my birthday! Yay Limos and Arik!<br /><br />One thing that I noticed was that Eternal Rider seemed quite similar to Passion Unleashed, and it reminded me of Wraith and Serena. Like Serena, Cara kept getting sicker and sicker and was what would affect the outcome of Ares' life like Serena did with Wraith. The only thing that was different was that Serena could have died, but Cara's death had to be prevented. <br /><br />So...yeah. I actually did like this book. I really, really did. I just...had some issues with Cara and that's what brought this review down in starage. I can't wait for Immortal Rider because Limos is my favorite Horseman and I can't wait to read about her and Arik.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11570095096592511998" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/123266660?book_show_action=true">Sep 24, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AH" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AH" href="/user/show/3255548-ah">AH</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=alpha-males">alpha-males</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=demons">demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=first-in-series">first-in-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=babr-reviews">babr-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=angels">angels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=zzread-nov-2011">zzread-nov-2011</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer123266660" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6197083193936045448">Awesome! I loved this!<br/><br/>I’m a sucker for books that take Biblical themes and build upon them. Angels, demons, images of heaven and hell, obscure Biblical and apocryphal stories – I love it. Larissa Ione’s Eternal Rider gives the story a modern flavor. The series builds upon the author’s Demonica series and is best read after Sin Undone. Many of the Demonica character favorites appear in this spin-off series.<br/><br/>Larissa Ione has superb storytelling skills. From the first page to the last, the book was </span>
  <span id="freeText6197083193936045448" style="display:none">Awesome! I loved this!<br /><br />I’m a sucker for books that take Biblical themes and build upon them. Angels, demons, images of heaven and hell, obscure Biblical and apocryphal stories – I love it. Larissa Ione’s Eternal Rider gives the story a modern flavor. The series builds upon the author’s Demonica series and is best read after Sin Undone. Many of the Demonica character favorites appear in this spin-off series.<br /><br />Larissa Ione has superb storytelling skills. From the first page to the last, the book was action-packed, fast paced, and full of sexual steaminess. I could not put this book down. The world building is spectacular. The reader is immersed in a world full of angels, demons, and other creatures all waging a war between good and evil. The battle scenes were extremely well done. I felt as if I were there. I enjoyed the author’s sense of humor. Her dialogues are witty and clever. Her use of acronyms makes me chuckle. Who else would name their hospital UGH – Underworld General Hospital?<br /><br />When it comes to writing alpha males, the author is in a class by herself. The descriptions of Ares had me swooning. I loved Ares and his love interest Cara. They were wonderful together.<br /> <br />Of course, the story can always be improved with the addition of a cute puppy. In this case, a cute hellhound named Hal, short for Halitosis. Best watchdog ever!<br /><br />If you haven't read Larissa Ione's Demonica series, I would suggest you start there, just to get a taste of her world. You can start with this book, but you may miss some of the fun stuff. <br /><br /><b>Check out my review on <a href="http://badassbookreviews.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Badass Book Reviews.</a></b><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

          </span>
        </div>

She is twisted and has this crazy "other world" so perfectly laid out that I am convinced that she is writing from experience rather than "make believe". <br/><br/>I'll review this later, right now, I'm just going to think about how much I enjoyed it!</span>

<div id="review_152155370" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/152155370" />
    <a title="Jen Davis" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis"><img alt="Jen Davis" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1548427639p2/4669344.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/152155370?book_show_action=true">Mar 04, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen Davis" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen Davis" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis">Jen Davis</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669344-jen-davis?shelf=arcs">arcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669344-jen-davis?shelf=pararnormal-romance">pararnormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669344-jen-davis?shelf=demonica">demonica</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer152155370" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8615551065445414349">The Demonica series may have ended with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7715664.Sin_Undone__Demonica___5_' title='Sin Undone (Demonica, #5) by Larissa Ione' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sin Undone</a>, but its rich world is very much alive thanks to Larissa Ione's spinoff series Lords of Deliverance. Off the bat, I can tell you that you don't have to have read the Demonica books to enjoy Eternal Rider. While it doesn't build the world from scratch, our main characters have their own story to tell. <br/><br/>Let me give you the basics. There are four Horsemen of the Apocalypse. They're not bad guys. In fact, they want to be a force for good. But each ca</span>
  <span id="freeText8615551065445414349" style="display:none">The Demonica series may have ended with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7715664.Sin_Undone__Demonica___5_" title="Sin Undone (Demonica, #5) by Larissa Ione" rel="nofollow noopener">Sin Undone</a>, but its rich world is very much alive thanks to Larissa Ione's spinoff series Lords of Deliverance. Off the bat, I can tell you that you don't have to have read the Demonica books to enjoy Eternal Rider. While it doesn't build the world from scratch, our main characters have their own story to tell. <br /><br />Let me give you the basics. There are four Horsemen of the Apocalypse. They're not bad guys. In fact, they want to be a force for good. But each carries a seal, that if broken, will unleash his (or her) curse. The first Horseman, Pestilence, had his seal broken during the events of Sin Undone. Now he is hellbent on breaking the seals of his brothers and sister and bringing about the apocalypse. <br /><br />Ares is the Horseman of War. His seal is carried by a Fallen Angel. That seal will break if the angel dies. But it can be passed to someone else... which is what happens. A human, Cara, becomes the unwitting recipient. This throws her together with Ares, who has to protect her to protect his seal.<br /><br />It took me a little while to really get into the book. Ione's books are always richly layered and that takes time to establish. The great secondary characters and storylines have always heated up the page, even if the main characters needed time to stumble their way through the book to get together. Obviously, that didn't happen in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/2679633.Pleasure_Unbound__Demonica___1_" title="Pleasure Unbound (Demonica, #1) by Larissa Ione" rel="nofollow noopener">Pleasure Unbound</a>, but the sexual element was there in that one from the very beginning. Here, we have neither the luxury of a great secondary story (like Kynan &amp; Gem or Luc &amp; Kar gave us in previous installments) or the quick sexual relationship we were treated to with Tayla &amp; Eidolon. The result was something of a slow-build.<br /><br />Of course, when things begin to heat up, the second half of the book flies by. Ione does a great job putting sex on paper. A really great job. The tension is palpable between Ares and Cara... and the payoff is even better. Plus, those fantastic Demonica characters are back, albeit in supporting roles. It was wonderful to see our old friends again and revisit Underworld General Hospital. Ione has also laid the foundation for the next book in the series, centered on the female Horseman, Limos. My wheels are already spinning with ideas about what will happen next. 4 stars.<br /><br />*ARC Provided by Grand Central Publishing/Hachette Book Group</span>
  <a data-text-id="8615551065445414349" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_339799444" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/339799444" />
    <a title="new_user" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1365355-new-user"><img alt="new_user" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1351189841p2/1365355.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/339799444?book_show_action=true">May 30, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="new_user" class="user" itemprop="url" name="new_user" href="/user/show/1365355-new-user">new_user</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780749955427" href="/book/show/9598203-eternal-rider">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1365355-new-user?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer339799444" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15826197854425856213"><b>Larissa Ione stacked her <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/series/45381-demonica' target='new' rel='nofollow noopener'><i>Demonica</i></a> series on sympathetic men and women, a <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13636496.The_Demonica_Compendium' title='The Demonica Compendium by Larissa Ione' rel='nofollow noopener'>compendium-full</a> of demons neither sparkly nor vegetarian, twisty plots, violence, romance, and brotherly bonds that inspire bloodshed and manly half-hugs.<br/><br/>Which is why <i>Eternal Rider</i> disappointed me.</b><br/><br/>Ever ambitious, in her <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/series/51284-lords-of-deliverance' target='new' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <i>Lords of Deliverance</i>
</a> quintet, Ione attacks the biblical four horsemen of the Apocalypse. <br/><br/>It was violent at least. When catastrophe strikes, magically warping affable horseman Reseph to villain, his broth</span>
  <span id="freeText15826197854425856213" style="display:none"><b>Larissa Ione stacked her <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/45381-demonica" target="new" rel="nofollow noopener"><i>Demonica</i></a> series on sympathetic men and women, a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13636496.The_Demonica_Compendium" title="The Demonica Compendium by Larissa Ione" rel="nofollow noopener">compendium-full</a> of demons neither sparkly nor vegetarian, twisty plots, violence, romance, and brotherly bonds that inspire bloodshed and manly half-hugs.<br /><br />Which is why <i>Eternal Rider</i> disappointed me.</b><br /><br />Ever ambitious, in her <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/51284-lords-of-deliverance" target="new" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <i>Lords of Deliverance</i>
</a> quintet, Ione attacks the biblical four horsemen of the Apocalypse. <br /><br />It was violent at least. When catastrophe strikes, magically warping affable horseman Reseph to villain, his brothers, Ares and Thanatos, and his sister, Limos, must stop his crimes and prevent Armageddon. Reseph as Pestilence exploits a cruel imagination, and the horsemen cannot technically die, so stuff gets bloody.<br /><br />Pestilence and co. clash with male lead Ares here or there, but love interest Cara says it best. When an angel asks her if she's having difficulty reconciling his existence, she scoffs, "I'm sitting in a room with the second Horseman of the Apocalypse." Girlfriend ain't kidding. She sits in that room for the entire book. When Ares and Cara reach his Greek villa, they don't leave. Picturesque Greek getaways have no place in apocalyptic novels, ladies and gentlemen. <br /><br />But NU! you say. If not action, then character development? I could summarize Cara and Ares' respective baggage in two lines. (I won't.) We didn't need an endless pitstop. <br /><br />Ares himself disappointed me. Ione excels at writing characters that we imagine relaxing and watching an episode of <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Grimm_%28TV_series%29" target="new" rel="nofollow noopener">Grimm</a> with us. She didn't need to resort to the caveman alpha, and Ares suffers the same problem as any rake in fiction. He's lapped the block so many times, it's unbelievable when he settles with a doe. Those people die of syphillis, m'kay? <br /><br />Cara's growth spurt from shrinking violet to... something else, stretched credibility too, especially when she attributes that to Ares. Ares didn't support her. He couldn't have made her stronger, unless you believe in the school of hard knocks. I would have liked her stronger, minus the trite Oh-noes-I-killed-in-self-defense episode. Where's <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/characters/49628-chess-putnam" rel="nofollow noopener">Chess</a> when you need her? She's another soft and ever so gentle Girl Healer archetype. <br /><br />Finally, Ares interacted with two brothers and a sister, but I missed the family element. I don't know if I was missing the sibling ribbings or if the horsemen just seemed too inhuman. That's the problem with near-godly, done-everything-in-existence characters. <br /><br />That was harsh. I'll say Ares appealed more when he finally developed, y'know, emotions, in the last quarter after knocking boots, and the moments when the horsemen's familial feelings did arise, e.g. Limos thinking about her brothers. Also the Seminus' bros cameos. Also the cover! Dude on a horse. From the <a href="http://www.google.com/url?sa=t&amp;rct=j&amp;q=i%27m%20on%20a%20horse&amp;source=web&amp;cd=1&amp;ved=0CGcQtwIwAA&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv%3DowGykVbfgUE&amp;ei=9kvaT4GZCoqA2wWa-qmsBg&amp;usg=AFQjCNHwC-kM_0WRpj9qNpl5xw8hTOVl6A&amp;cad=rja" target="new" rel="nofollow noopener">Isaiah Mustafa</a> Guide to Success. <br /><br />In short, read this if you love <a href="http://www.imdb.com/title/tt0800369/" rel="nofollow noopener">Thor</a> and long walks on the beach. LOL. Two stars. Now. I REQUIRE SUSTENANCE!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15826197854425856213" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/99653132" />
    <a title="valee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2320890-valee"><img alt="valee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1443365004p2/2320890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/99653132?book_show_action=true">Apr 22, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="valee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="valee" href="/user/show/2320890-valee">valee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780749955427" href="/book/show/9598203-eternal-rider">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2320890-valee?shelf=amazing-pnr-romance">amazing-pnr-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2320890-valee?shelf=fav-series-and-reads">fav-series-and-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer99653132" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7466101857432400763">4.5 STARS<br/><br/>There's ONLY ONE reason for why I'm only giving 4 stars to this book and it's because I have NO DOUBT WHATSOEVER that <b>this series will only get better,</b> and in a way I feel I only want to use the 5 stars once that happens. For a first book in a series it couldn't have been better, although if it had been longer and with more information about the other Lords maybe it could have,LOL.<br/><br/><b>SOME THOUGHTS ABOUT THIS AMAZING AUTHOR:</b><br/>Again I remember why I admire this author so much: I believe Lariss</span>
  <span id="freeText7466101857432400763" style="display:none">4.5 STARS<br /><br />There's ONLY ONE reason for why I'm only giving 4 stars to this book and it's because I have NO DOUBT WHATSOEVER that <b>this series will only get better,</b> and in a way I feel I only want to use the 5 stars once that happens. For a first book in a series it couldn't have been better, although if it had been longer and with more information about the other Lords maybe it could have,LOL.<br /><br /><b>SOME THOUGHTS ABOUT THIS AMAZING AUTHOR:</b><br />Again I remember why I admire this author so much: I believe Larissa Ione has become one of the best authors in this genre. Not only does she have one of the best sense of humors out there but she is capable of giving us so much more than the other authors in this genre. Her books are not only some science fiction, a bit of romance and hot scenes all mixed up, she goes so much more beyond that. With every book written by her we get an amazing plot (which will get us hooked till the end without being able to stop or read it slow, even if you want or need to), the best characters ever (which are so very different between each other that you get to feel you actually get to know them more and more with every page, like they were real) and too many amazing laughs. But more than all that, what I adore the most about this author is the way she has to create a WHOLE NEW world from scratch. While reading her books, we don't think about any other series we have read, that's because there just are't similar series out there, her's is just so original that you can't help to love it (I'm talking about her Demonica and Lords of Deliverance series as they are both set in the same world).<br /><br />I just know that everything written by this author will be read and recommended by me because there's no way Larissa Ione can write something I don't end up loving it.<br /><br /><b>SOME THOUGHTS ABOUT THE BOOK:</b><br />I don't even know what to say! I just loved it, an amazing beginning to a series that seem it can only get more interesting and addicting. I really can't wait for the next installment. The romance was amazing as well as the plot. Although here is the reason I didn't give a higher rating to the book, I did feel like the plot and the character could have been better developed. I would have LOVED to read a longer book about this 2 main characters. I also felt like much more could have been explained about this 4 siblings and their history as have lived for so long. The whole time I wanted to know them better but I never felt like I did. With the Demonica books I always felt I got to know so well the characters I could never get them confused. In this book I felt this was missing a bit, I would have loved to see more glimpses of the siblings personalities.Also the bad guy being one of the brothers was kind of a bummer as it reminded me of the Demonica series. I would have definitely prefer they helped him become one of the good guys again and finding a new enemy to fight against, I love the family bonds that we get to see between the characters in Larissa's books and I don't want to see one of the brothers as one of the bad guys AGAIN. <br /><br />But apart from this minor things the book was astonishing and I couldn't put it down.I know next book can only get better and I can't wait. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7466101857432400763" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_145347964" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/145347964" />
    <a title="Mandi Schreiner" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2704703-mandi-schreiner"><img alt="Mandi Schreiner" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368979996p2/2704703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/145347964?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mandi Schreiner" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mandi Schreiner" href="/user/show/2704703-mandi-schreiner">Mandi Schreiner</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2704703-mandi-schreiner?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer145347964" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5006600073895107914">Let’s all jump for joy – Larissa Ione has a new series out. Her Demonica series is one of my favorites, not only for the super sexy romance, but her humorous, warm characters. I am so glad that although set in the same world as Demonica, we have four new main characters with the same wit and sexy behavior. Now, although this is a spin-off series, there are a lot of new rules we have to learn. Demons are not the main focus of this one, the Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse are in the spotlight. Are</span>
  <span id="freeText5006600073895107914" style="display:none">Let’s all jump for joy – Larissa Ione has a new series out. Her Demonica series is one of my favorites, not only for the super sexy romance, but her humorous, warm characters. I am so glad that although set in the same world as Demonica, we have four new main characters with the same wit and sexy behavior. Now, although this is a spin-off series, there are a lot of new rules we have to learn. Demons are not the main focus of this one, the Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse are in the spotlight. Ares (War), Reseph (Pestilence), Thanatos (Death), and the only girl of the group, Limos (Famine). Each of the Horsemen have a Seal and each Seal comes with two prophecies. Don’t let the Seal break, and save the world. But if the Seal does break, it will be the end of the world. Unfortunately, Reseph’s Seal broke and the once good natured brother, is now reveling in causing disease and plagues throughout the world.<br /><br />Cara gets dragged into the mess when an injured dog lands on her doorstep. Although not a practicing vet, she has a secret magical ability to heal animals, although it scares her to use it. But this dog is no ordinary dog – it is actually a hellhound puppy that unknown to her, bonds with her. Through a series of events, the unfallen angel that is carrying Ares’ seal, passes it to Cara. A human isn’t suppose to be strong enough to carry Seals, but because she is bonded to the hellhound, she is alive – for now. Ares must make sure Cara stays alive, or he his Seal will break and he will become “War.”<br /><br />It took me a good bit to get into this book. Like I said, it is set in Demonica’s world, but there are so many new rules we have to learn. I honestly became a little overwhelmed at the beginning with the information overload. But, Larissa Ione does a nice job throughout the book reminding you of all the rules, that my advice is to just plow your way through the beginning, because it works out that you won’t be lost. I love that the Horsemen have the capacity to become these very evil beings, and when triggered, their curses start to come out –yet they really are fighting on the side of good. And even better, the Aegis, who is a human group who protects the world from demons, etc… have this ambiguous role in the book. Even though they are here to protect Earth, many times they ultimately do things to hurt events put in motion by the Horsemen. The lines of good vs. evil are blurred and it really makes it to be an interesting aspect of the book.<br /><br />One person who is truly evil is Reseph (who turned into Pestilence). He is violent, horrible, and unforgiving. And I assume he eventually must turn around and become good and get his own book (or so I hope) and I’m dying to see how this happens. Right now he is totally unredeemable. And I love it.<br /><br />Ares and Cara have a nice build up to their romance, and per Larissa Ione style, very nice sex scenes. The action is great and the supporting characters all play nice roles. We see lots of Demonica characters as well- Reaver (an angel who is a “watcher” of the Horsemen) Kynan and Arik. Eidolen and Wraith each have a small role as well.<br /><br />Overall, a nice start to this new series. Very excited about the rest of the siblings, especially with Limos up next!<br /><br />Rating: B</span>
  <a data-text-id="5006600073895107914" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
